Scratched versions for a bit less.  Free shipping.  Highly rated seller.  For $180, the 10th gen version is also available.  There's an ebay $10 off coupon today.

I re-use old cases, old PSUs, old speakers, provided each works like new still.  My 5.1 speakers are over 20 yrs old now. Cases are 25 yrs old.  Think the last PSU I bought was in 2008.  My desktop is rated just under 20,000 passmarks. It replaced a powerful MB/CPU rated around 6000 passmarks that used 2x the power.  The cost of the new system was paid for by lower electric bills in less than 3 yrs of running. Add in my "increased happiness" and it was a huge win.

    â†³  @Ottertiles  ğŸ‘0  2025-03-12
    Original: @alanbo859Â  It is a tough decision because our interests are different. But because I am an engineering student I can relate to you. Let's break it down:

1. Macbook M3 pro: good if you get it at 16/512. It will be heavy especially for a laptop to carry around. It has a fan that can handle a lot of phyton, js, or simulation better than a fanless laptop. It has more battery which is a big deal.

2. Macbook Air M4: my judgment is a bit biased cuz I like to move around and get my job done outside. It will serve some improvement I believe from the previous chip and give you more portability.

3. The RTX laptop has two categories now, the lightweight like Zenbook and the chunky Bigboy like ROG, Legion, and Katana. Please make sure to get the x86 manufacturer just for more compatibility for developers. Laptops with RTX Will give you more raw power in exchange for battery life. 

a. I preferably will choose the lightweight Zenbook because it can last at least close to the Macbook. It is a bit biased because I love to move around which laptop battery is a big deal for me and also its performance.

b. If you want to get raw power but it's okay with 3-4 hours of battery life and a jet engine then it's chunky. Or seriously just get a PC, I can't survive in the wild with that kinda battery and jet engine.

Conclusion: I will recommend you the MacBook Air M4. Apple silicon will eat your everyday project like a piece of cake while giving you a long battery life. It is supposed to have a ray tracing same as M3 so js or Blender will be easy. If you're into machine learning and data mining get the M3 Pro, because of the fan. Or if you live in Canada just toss your laptop outside the fan or no fan no problem ğŸ˜‚

I hope this will help you make the decision.

    â†³ âœ… @jpflu3754  ğŸ‘0  2025-03-27
    Original: @chargersfan1111 Definitely an impressive CPU.  Apple knew that changing from Intel compatibility to a proprietary chip would have pros and cons.  Running a different CPU means having a different instruction set and that emulating other platforms would be a little harder.  Having much of the system in a single chip, also called an SBC - Single Board Computer - reduces manufacturing costs and locks people into their products more than using generally available CPUs does.  

A bunch of people would buy the Apple hardware, but wipe MacOS from it and run other OSes when it was Intel-based.  Apple usually makes good, long-lasting, hardware.
    Sentiment: positive (confidence 0.67)
